Tuis
set
of
four
books
of
problems
is

on
a
translation
of
a
Russian
collection
which
has
been
in
use
by

in

Moscow
State

and
the
Moscow
Physico
Technical
In
stitute
for
a
number
of
years
Where

and

to
the
problems
are

in
the
second
part
of
each
volume
During

course
of
the
translation
of
these
volumes
the
authors
provided
a
large
list
of

and

to
their
Russian

and
these

all

incorporated
in
this
English
edition
Many
ofthe
additional
problems
are
on
topics
which
have
developed
during
recent
years
The
standard
of
the
problems
is
roughly
equivalent
to
an
undergraduate
degree
course
in
physics
at
a
British
university
or
at
an
American
university
it
varies
from
the
simple

rather

They
can

used

with

any

on
physics
at
the
appropriate
level
